  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_8a6255b9-17f2-4528-a125-0c620d14df54'
      });

  <span id="freeText16112216884237797212" style="display:none">NOTE FROM THE AUTHOR: This book is no longer available from Dreamspinner Press (the audio version and translations still are). Forced to work together to survive, the two men forge a bond that ripens into unexpected passion. Jack sees the wounded soul beneath D's cold, detached exterior, and D finds in Jack the person who can help him reclaim the man he once was. <br /><br />As the day of Jack's testimony approaches, he and D find themselves not only fighting for their lives... but also fighting for their future. <a href="/questions/960625-does-it-end-on-a-cliffhanger-because-it">Does it end on a cliffhanger ? Because it says its part of a series but there are no other books.</a>
</div>
<div class='communityQAFooter questionFooter'>
<ul class='questionFooterActions'>
<li class='footerItem like'>
<span class='likeItContainer' id='like_container_community_question_960625'><a rel="nofollow" class="jsLike like_it" href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/new?remember=true&amp;return_url=%2Fbook%2Fshow%2F6382879-zero-at-the-bone">like</a></span>

<div class='answererUserIcon'>
<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/45877708-destiny-jardin"><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/users/1555642611i/45877708._UX100_CR0,0,100,100_.jpg" /></a>
</div>
<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/45877708-destiny-jardin">Destiny Jardin</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">I believe it depends on what you define as "cliffhanger". And I've never seen anywhere that said it was part of a series, but the author did say she w<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">I believe it depends on what you define as "cliffhanger". And I've never seen anywhere that said it was part of a series, but the author did say she wanted to write a sequel, but we've yet to see it. The author does however have a website (<a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.janesevillebooks.com">http://www.janesevillebooks.com</a>) where she's posted a few free short stories as follow ups, along with a short novella that you can pay I believe $1.99 for called "A Very D Christmas". I've read them all and think they're definitely worth a look.<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>
</div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer734012444" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18087042525741061166"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428972519i/14509744.jpg' alt='' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>OK, so I was <b>SO INCREDIBLY LATE</b> to this party, it is almost shameful. <i>Zero at the Bone</i> was published way, way back in 2009. If you are a M/M romance fan, like me, and haven't read this FAN-FUCKING-TASTIC novel yet... <i>What are you waiting for?</i> I kept thinking that as I read this one: "I can't believe I am just reading this now!" And what is even <i>more</i> shameful? I bought this back in <a href='http://www.fredfarm.com/zeroscreenshot.jpg' rel='nofollow noopener'>January of 2012</a>! I am ridiculous.	<br/><br/>Mercenary MC "D" is a lost and lonely man. He has been denying his basic human emo</span>
  <span id="freeText18087042525741061166" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428972519i/14509744.jpg" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>OK, so I was <b>SO INCREDIBLY LATE</b> to this party, it is almost shameful. <i>Zero at the Bone</i> was published way, way back in 2009. If you are a M/M romance fan, like me, and haven't read this FAN-FUCKING-TASTIC novel yet... <i>What are you waiting for?</i> I kept thinking that as I read this one: "I can't believe I am just reading this now!" And what is even <i>more</i> shameful? I bought this back in <a href="http://www.fredfarm.com/zeroscreenshot.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener">January of 2012</a>! I am ridiculous.	<br><br>Mercenary MC "D" is a lost and lonely man. He has been denying his basic human emotions for 10 years, putting them in a "vault" that is locked up tight, and no one has the key. His most recent <u>target</u>, MC Dr. Jack Francisco, who's only crime was being at the wrong place at the wrong time, barrels into his life, picking away at the lock on D's vault. <br><br>A hit man and a surgeon? Really? <i>Really</i>.	<br><br>The sex is off-the-charts, the passion is glorious, the hurt/healing/comfort is the stuff of my wildest dreams and the story line? Blew me away! The way <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2892465.Jane_Seville" title="Jane Seville" rel="nofollow noopener">Jane Seville</a> actually pulled off a plausible way for these men to be attracted to each other was impressive enough. But to give them the rainbows and bird's singing HEA they eventually got? Fuck! Perfection! <br><br>Enough of my praise-vomit. This one is on my <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/list/11550843?shelf=fuck-yeah-5-plus-stars" rel="nofollow noopener">Fuck Yeah, 5+ Stars shelf</a> and it is the best of the best. If you haven't read this one yet, give yourself a nice block of time and start. This one does <b>NOT</b> disappoint.	 <br><br><b>HIGHLY RECOMMENDED!!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1428972519ra/14509745.gif" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="18087042525741061166" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_200484268" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/200484268" />
    <a title="Baba  " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4669232-baba"><img alt="Baba  " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1564910043p2/4669232.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/200484268?book_show_action=true">Aug 20, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Baba  " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Baba  " href="/user/show/4669232-baba">Baba  </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4669232-baba?shelf=m-m">m-m</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4669232-baba?shelf=memorable-favorite-heroes">memorable-favorite-heroes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4669232-baba?shelf=five-star-reads">five-star-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4669232-baba?shelf=military-and-former-mil-cia-navy">military-and-former-mil-cia-navy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4669232-baba?shelf=all-time-favorite-heroes">all-time-favorite-heroes</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer200484268" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17526654632896417390"><b>New review posted May 13, 2013*****Re-read and buddy read with Rosalinda, May 2013. Thank you, Rosa, it was a pleasure! *mwah*</b><br/> <br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380357310i/708630.jpg' alt=' photo ba00a080-bd0d-45e8-9a95-8a8b0fe18a35_zps9276c6da.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/> <br/>Jack is a maxillofacial surgeon with a subspecialty in craniofacial surgery. Maxillofacial surgeons treat injuries, diseases, and defects in the skull, jaw, neck, and face. After witnessing a mob hit in an underground garage, Jack is put into protective custody to keep him alive until the trial begins and he can testify. D is a hit man and a former <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[member</span></span>
  <span id="freeText17526654632896417390" style="display:none"><b>New review posted May 13, 2013*****Re-read and buddy read with Rosalinda, May 2013. Thank you, Rosa, it was a pleasure! *mwah*</b><br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380357310i/708630.jpg" alt=" photo ba00a080-bd0d-45e8-9a95-8a8b0fe18a35_zps9276c6da.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>Jack is a maxillofacial surgeon with a subspecialty in craniofacial surgery. Maxillofacial surgeons treat injuries, diseases, and defects in the skull, jaw, neck, and face. After witnessing a mob hit in an underground garage, Jack is put into protective custody to keep him alive until the trial begins and he can testify. D is a hit man and a former <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[member of a Special Forces unit. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> D’s credo is to kill bad people who deserve to die and Jack sure doesn’t fall into this category since he was an innocent bystander as well as a very important witness. Though the hit is contrary to D’s beliefs, he must accept it because he’s been blackmailed into killing Jack. Tracking Jack down is a piece of cake for D. Once there, however, D is struck by his conscience, and instead of killing him, D “kidnaps” Jack to protect him with his own life.<br> <br>Now they are on the run and are forced to work together to survive this thrilling and dangerous journey. For more than ten years D had only trusted one person but in his heart he wanted to trust Jack, and yet it scared him because trust can be misused easily. Though when Jack unravels D and can see the ‘real’ man beneath his cold exterior, D begins to yearn for something more than his harsh and lonely life as a hit man. Even though D suppressed his needs, wants, desires, and dreams Jack helped him to reclaim the man he once was. While on the run, these two men forge a strong bond that develops into a deep yet unexpected love that could weather any misgivings.<br> <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I'm not going anywhere with you."<br>"D'you have a fuckin' death wish?" HAL hissed at him. "Those fuckers are gonna come after me fer not killin' you, and they're gonna come after you fer not bein' dead yet, and no one can protect you from them! No one, ya hear? Not the Marshals, not the police, not the goddamned Neighborhood Watch! Yer only shot is ta stick with me!"</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380357310ra/708631.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m934eaZ8jK1ralk39o1_500_zpsd51754c8.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I'm sorry," Francisco snapped. "I've just never met a professional killer before, and I'm having a little trouble with the degrees of morality here." He sat back in his seat, exhaling. "I guess I shouldn't judge. Your rules saved my life, didn't they?"<br>"Reckon so."<br>A few tense minutes passed until Francisco sighed and his shoulders sagged. "I'm…"<br>"Don't worry about it," D said, cutting him off. "Yer right. I am bad folks."<br>Francisco said nothing for a few beats. "I don't think you're bad," he murmured.<br> <br>"Look, it must be real nice and comfy on top a that high horse," D said, suddenly snarling, "but you ain't lived in my world and it's jus' fine fer you ta judge when you don't gotta make them kinda choices."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380357310ra/708632.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m7gw127x3S1rsn15ao1_500_zpsf43d86a7.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>Loved D’s sense of humor.<br> <br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Holy shit," Jack said. "Are we taking over a small country?"<br>D snorted. "Gotta be prepared." He looked up at Jack's face, frowning. "What?"<br>Jack shrugged. "It's just…" He sighed. "I'm starting to see words like 'accessory' and 'accomplice' floating around my head."<br>D barely reacted. "How about 'dead on arrival'? Ya like that better?"<br>Jack nodded, pressing his lips together. "Get more ammo. Ammo is good."<br> <br>"Ooh, she said, and pulled out her own binoculars.<br>D looked at her. "Hey!"<br>"What? You'd deny a hardworking girl a little eye candy?"<br>"This ain't Halloween."<br>"What's that mean?"<br>"Means I ain't sharin' my candy. Gimme them glasses."<br> <br>"(…)Let me give you another shot--"<br>"Another one? My ass ain't no pincushion."<br>"For prophylaxis."<br>"Prophyl-whatsis? Ain't that a condom? What the hell you plannin', doc?"<br>Jack chuckled. "Prophylaxis is any preventative measure, like flossing to prevent gum disease. Condoms are sometimes called 'prophylactics" because they're a preventive measure against insemination.(…)"</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br> <br>The book title is pretty intriguing. It comes from the poem <i>Snake</i> by Emily Dickinson. Besides, the fact that Jack is a maxillofacial surgeon could also be related to the title. Jack specializes in facial reconstructive surgery. When Jack performs a surgery he can ‘see’ the bone structure beneath the patient’s face. Also, as this story unfolds, I got the impression that Jack is reassembling the ‘real’ person within D. Plus, Jack is incredibly fascinated by D's architectural skull and his bone structure.<br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/646407.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mdqsk0Qa331rjixpqo1_500_zps272ee806.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Jack shifted a little closer on the couch and spoke softly. "You thought if you could keep the dark away from me, that maybe some of it would leave you too."<br>D turned to look at him, and Jack saw something naked and exposed in his expression, set free by the <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[narcotics. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> That stoniness was gone, and Jack could see the child D had once been, and the <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[father, and the husband. The young soldier, the hopeful family man, <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> and it damned near broke his heart to see that man buried so deeply within the man D was now, a man he clearly detested but could not escape. His eyes were wide and shining. "I cain't remember what things look like without it," he said, his voice hoarse and shaky.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380357310i/708633.png" alt=" photo Bildschirmfoto2013-05-11um113008_zps765d40d0.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>He just persisted, touching D where he'd like to be touched, caressing the tension from his muscles, urging him on with his hands, trying to tell him with his body it's okay, it's okay to want me, it's okay to feel it, it's safe to show it.<br> <br>D was pouring himself into Jack's arms, his body, and the deluge was fierce; Jack clung to him like a barnacle, holding him fast in his arms. I've got you. I've got you. I've got you. The thought ran over and over in his mind as D heaved great swoops of breath past Jack's ear, swoops that had sobs caught at their dregs, as if he'd found something old and unexpressed at the very tidal bottom of his lungs now dragged into the open air by the exertion.<br>I'm not letting go of you.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380357310ra/708634.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mlslteDshg1r8xv9uo1_500_zps16b68992.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>D's features tugged inward, like he'd just remembered something. Jack didn't move. D blinked a few times, and then slowly leaned closer, lowering his face toward the crook of Jack's shoulder. Brow furrowed, he inhaled. Jack saw his eyes flutter closed and his features smooth out as if he were falling asleep right where he stood, falling into a daydream or a memory.<br>"Oh," he sighed, long and weary, the sight of sinking into a favorite chair after long hours of standing. "Ya smell like sun," he murmured. D's voice was raw, like a man under hypnosis. "Ya know that smell? That toasty-skin smell, like ya get after goin' ta the beach?" He nodded a little. "I love that smell."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380357310i/708635.png" alt=" photo Bildschirmfoto2013-05-12um183727_zps294437ea.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Jack, I…I dunno how--"<br>"It's okay. Take your time."<br>"I gotta tell ya…" He trailed off again.<br>"I know."<br>"Don't…don't let go a me." This last was so quiet as to almost be inaudible.<br>"I won't. Not ever."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380357310ra/708636.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m57corJmhc1r1985no1_500_zpsf3379f10.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You're not the last man on Earth. Not now."<br>D stared at him, his eyes misting over. Two tears spilled over his lids and slid down his cheek. Jack wiped them away with his thumbs and leaned forward until their foreheads were pressed together. He could hear D's ragged breathing; he felt another solitary tear drip onto his leg. How long had it been since this man had allowed himself an emotional release? How far could he really expect him to come back in one night?</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380357310i/708637._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo c00a48b1-516f-411a-851c-8fcafe29aeab_zpsa02f1d04.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>Hot damn! I forgot how fabulous this book is! Back in May 2011 I popped my M/M cherry with Zero and I am super duper happy to tell you that my re-read was so worthy of my time. A few weeks ago I removed it from my all-time favorites shelf (don’t ask me why I did that), but it’s right back where it belongs. Zero features fantastic MCs and an interesting cast of secondary characters. A solid plot, great dialogue and some intense men lovin’ kept my interest throughout the whole book. There sure was not one single dull moment to be found. Zero is an intense and wonderful love story. Honestly, the writing is excellent and some paragraphs are stunningly beautiful. Behind all the harshness and violence of the plot as well as D's character, something incredibly intimate and tender is hidden and needs to be unraveled. The build-up is rather slow yet beautifully done and the story provides many, many memorable scenes between D and Jack. I marvel at the beauty of anything and everything that Zero provides. I truly loved it! In fact, it was even better the second time around.<br> <br>More often than not I get annoyed by too much narrative and inner monologue. Funnily enough, that’s exactly what I loved about Zero because the author is so incredibly skilled and kept D’s internal tensions and struggles palpable and engaging through exceptionally good narrative and inner monologue. D’s heart-breaking background story shaped him into the man he is today, but there is always hope for a change. Hope to live a ‘normal’ life again. D is ‘damaged goods’, with a tortured soul and heart, and he is void of emotions and feelings. I think the author conveyed his guilt with an intense clarity of thought and offered the reader a very intimate look inside a criminal’s mind, who despite everything, still has a conscience. In fact, the man was standing at a personal crossroads and wanted to seek redemption eventually. Hence, Zero is not only a simple love story, it’s so much more. Jack seemed to be the trigger to D’s personal atonement, because in the end D could only feel worthy of Jack’s love after having achieved atonement to a certain extent. Also, <b>Zero lives and breathes intimacy,</b> and I truly adored the moments of utter stillness and tenderness. On the other hand, however, the lovely, tender and vulnerable moments went hand in hand with frantic lovemaking that was truly stunning. Besides, I was privy to the privilege of witnessing D coming completely and utterly undone and Jack was right there to hold him. He wouldn’t let him go. Ever.<br> <br>For the last ten years D acted like a machine, he did avoid any emotional attachment to every human being. He didn’t even know what love is. And then slowly yet steadily D is flooded by so many confusing emotions and a never ending yearning for Jack. A yearning that hurt in its intensity, and yet it helped to keep the tension between these two very palpable. As a matter of fact, the sexual tension between Jack and D is extremely well done. Not every author is able to convey the physical attraction through words in such a powerful way like Jane Seville did in this story. And while the sex wasn’t overly hot or explicit, the beautiful prose and their mutual longing, need and passion made it so incredibly sexy and sensual. I felt like all of their feelings leapt right off the pages and into my heart, and I treasured those moments immensely. D and Jack are perfect together, but I believe that D totally made this story. I loved his character to pieces, and his accent endeared him even more to me.<br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380357310ra/708638.gif" alt=" photo large_zpsf7f19344.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>Now <i>that</i> inner monologue made me cry.<br> <br><blockquote>
  <i>Jus hold me a little longer, Jack. Tell me again that ya wanna be with me, fer real, cross yer heart 'n' let me know you ain't foolin' cause I dunno how or when it happen but somehow I come ta need ya like air, like blood. Touch me again like ya do with them gentle hands make me feel like somethin' precious. Say it again that ya love me, cause hearin' that was like openin' up some big bottomless well that ran dry years back and it cain't never hear it enough, but once more, one more time and maybe I'll believe it a little more, and then a little more the next time, till someday I believe it fer true enough ta be able to say it back ta you like y'oughta hear it said cause God knows I love you more'n my own life, more'n anythin' in this world, but it cain't get outta me yet cause I still ain't the man I need ta be, the man who's gonna stand before you and declare.</i>
</blockquote><br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380357310ra/708639.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mfnn0m2Enw1rmdeaso1_500_zps31cdde53.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br> <br>Zero at the Bone is a book full of heart, emotion, passion, beauty, and soul. Read it.<br> </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="17526654632896417390" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/445581030?book_show_action=true">Oct 31, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/6393872-zero-at-the-bone">review of another edition</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer445581030" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer6658202487367997567"><b>Why doesn't this author write MORE?!?! I adored this book! Jane Seville just BLEW MY MIND!</b><br/><br/>There are so many amazing reviews of this book by many of my Goodreads friends. A few days have gone by since I have read this book and the characters and their chemistry are still with me. I'm having trouble organizing my thoughts so I'll just blurt out a few highlights:<br/><br/>1) Can I just say how much I love that Jack was an oral surgeon?! As someone who really knows and understands oral surgery, I think that t</span>
  <span id="freeText6658202487367997567" style="display:none"><b>Why doesn't this author write MORE?!?! I adored this book! Jane Seville just BLEW MY MIND!</b><br /><br />There are so many amazing reviews of this book by many of my Goodreads friends. A few days have gone by since I have read this book and the characters and their chemistry are still with me. I'm having trouble organizing my thoughts so I'll just blurt out a few highlights:<br /><br />1) Can I just say how much I love that Jack was an oral surgeon?! As someone who really knows and understands oral surgery, I think that the author did a kick butt job of accurately describing the profession and the training involved. I felt like I connected with the character based on this alone (though I know I'm crazy biased). I automatically loved him because he was a dentist- I couldn't help myself!<br /><br />2) I don't know why but I have a thing for grunty, quiet, reticent main characters so, of course, D was amazing for my tastes. I loved how you really got to see him fall apart and let Jack in, emotionally. It was beautiful to read.<br /><br />3) This author has a serious way with words. She describes things so gorgeously and skillfully that I really felt like I was there with the guys, going through the action with them. I loved her style and it really enhanced my reading experience. <br /><br />What would I have improved? I didn't love the epilogue and I think some of the sex scenes could have really used more description (like about 100 pages of excruciating detail!!). I also wanted more character description: I couldn't picture the two MCs well at all. I didn't even know that D had light hair until the end of the book. However, the positives far outweigh the negatives here. Amazing book Ms. Seville!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="6658202487367997567" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_285458127" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/285458127" />
    <a title="Monique" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6875778-monique"><img alt="Monique" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1584362433p2/6875778.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/285458127?book_show_action=true">Feb 28, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Monique" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Monique" href="/user/show/6875778-monique">Monique</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6875778-monique?shelf=lgbt">lgbt</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer285458127" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10585909209688301025"><b>This book was incredibly well written by Jane Seville and has all the ingredients for a great read....action, kidnapping, courtroom drama, car chases, shoot outs, a big dose of humour and a beautifully told romance between two very unlikely characters.</b><br/><br/><b>5 Glorious Stars</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1166.photobucket.com/albums/q618/Monique_Lehane/Issac%20Jones/?action=view&current=tumblr_m80kg2KDKp1rubwz4o1_500-1.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380371019i/724001._SY540_.jpg' alt='Issac Jones' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>We meet Dr. Jack Francisco in a Police interview room, still covered in the blood of a woman he saw murdered, before his very eyes.....Maria Dominguez. She was due to testify against her ex husband, one of the Dominguez Brothers</span>
  <span id="freeText10585909209688301025" style="display:none"><b>This book was incredibly well written by Jane Seville and has all the ingredients for a great read....action, kidnapping, courtroom drama, car chases, shoot outs, a big dose of humour and a beautifully told romance between two very unlikely characters.</b><br><br><b>5 Glorious Stars</b><br><br><a href="http://s1166.photobucket.com/albums/q618/Monique_Lehane/Issac%20Jones/?action=view&amp;current=tumblr_m80kg2KDKp1rubwz4o1_500-1.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380371019i/724001._SY540_.jpg" alt="Issac Jones" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>We meet Dr. Jack Francisco in a Police interview room, still covered in the blood of a woman he saw murdered, before his very eyes.....Maria Dominguez. She was due to testify against her ex husband, one of the Dominguez Brothers for his part in the Brothers illegal drug trade operation. In this underworld of crime...all threats are illiminated.<br><br>Jack was scared....very scared. Sitting in a room with faceless, suited men, bombarding him with questions, repeating the same answers over and over again, he is confused and bewildered. He is about to be whisked away into witness protection....to become anonymous, to become a nobody. Checked out of his previous life as a top surgeon which he had trained for and worked hard to achieve. All his dreams and future life would be gone.....He has witnessed a crime and with all his well meant notions of good verses evil, he was prepared to stand up for what was right and testify and so far, HE, was still alive.....but for how long?<br><br>D is an assassin, a hired cold blooded killer. He has no past. He has no name. He has no life. He is like a machine and performs like a robot, without feeling or concern. He gets a hit, does the hit, moves on......simple! Mmmmm....except he does have a code, no kids, no women and no innocents. So when his handler asks him to take the hit on Jack and he refuses...someone else has other plans and blackmails D into taking it!<br><br>So our two MC's meet. Jack, in witness protection, on a never ending loop of boredom filled with mind numbing nothing-ness, goes hiking to relieve the tedium, try to exhaust himself to escape the futility of it all. Arriving home he finds a man, sitting in a chair in the shadows (heart was pounding at this point, all kinds of "Oh No" and expletives, entering my head). When he, cool as you like, stands slowly all quiet menace and deadly intent, lanky frame, shorn hair, stubble and sunglasses! inside.....really! (OK at this point I was drooling and open mouthed in anticipation) Jack knows he is going to die and surprisingly embraces it, as he no longer has to live in fear of it.......So, OK, we know he does't go through with it, as that would be the end of the story!!<br><br>Jack is fascinated by D and his analytical brain wanted answers, he wanted to know what was beneath that steely resolve. He should be afraid and in a way he was. But he had seen that small display of emotion from the man that had been hired to kill him, with his indecision when faced with the kill shot. So stilted and unemotional was D that Jack started referring to him as Hal (2001-Space Odyssey computer) in his mind. In fact Jack did a lot of talking to himself, arguing with himself, his inner monologue and musings were hilarious, and it was fun to watch his constant indecision.<br><br>As we see more of D we are let inside the complex gates and barriers he hides behind. He has a heart and Jack is slowly wearing those defences down, he can see beyond this persona that D has created and he doesn't see the coldness and the cruelty....there is more to D. Only D cannot see past the darkness and is unable to remember what life was like without it, he wants to protect Jack from it, he wants him to remain the kind, funny innocent man that he is.<br><br>The relationship evolves amongst all the madness and it is both beautiful and tender in all its complexities. It is fragile and tentative as D lets Jack in, past the barriers, to see the tragedy and hurt that have framed this man into "D" he slowly crawls out of the darkness and is desperate to keep hold of the man that trusts him and has opened his heart to what life can truly be like. <br><br>I loved this book, the voices of the two MC's are so distinct, their personalities were intense and so real, I could see them and hear them in my minds eye. I did struggle however with D's accent for the first few pages, unable to decipher it, but when I got the southern drawl, that was all 'D' their voices were perfect and I was on a roll.<br><br>Which brings me to my only gripe with regard to Zero. When I read I like to have an image and voice to go with the character, this is usually provided by the author with snippets of information at the beginning to help us build a picture of this person of persons in our mind. Even though we are given a full description of D's look, all drool-worthy and lusciousness that he is, the same is not true of Jack. We learn early on he has blue eyes..that's it! Later on towards the end we finally learn he has dark hair...that's it! Which also goes for the accent, which was OK for me but I know a few people have has issue with, if it was pointed out that D was a southern boy, it would all have been good.<br><br>There are some sex scenes in this book and the build up to them was amazing, all tummy flutters and anticipation, only to fall flat on the deed. My original theory, was that as the barriers were broken down, it would improve and it did slightly, but it was still all fired up to only deliver a sizzle. Having said that, this book is more about the emotional connection that develops over time, rather than the sex and that was all fine with me, even though I am sure a few of my pervy friends would say otherwise!!<br><br><a href="http://s1166.photobucket.com/albums/q618/Monique_Lehane/Issac%20Jones/?action=view&amp;current=Hunk_Issac_Jones_in_black_and_white.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380371019i/724002._SX540_.jpg" alt="Issac Jones" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="10585909209688301025" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

D has some strange accent and speaks jargon all the time, so it took me a while to get used to that too lol<br/><br/>So the story is about Jack, the doctor with the perfect life, witnessing a murder done by the mob, and of course, after he goes to the witness list they all want him dead.   <span id="freeText1540784266049667881" style="display:none"><b>This book is something like watching an action mafia movie, only it has more personal drama and gay heroes</b> <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=355146.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

D has some strange accent and speaks jargon all the time, so it took me a while to get used to that too lol<br><br>So the story is about Jack, the doctor with the perfect life, witnessing a murder done by the mob, and of course, after he goes to the witness list they all want him dead. D, the mysterious contract killer, is blackmailed into taking the hit to Jack. Although he's a killer, he can't bring himself to kill an innocent man, so he and Jack are forced to run together because they are both targets now.<br><br>It went really slow with them in the beginning, I was squealing all the time, just waiting for something to happen <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=311685.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<span id="freeTextContainer3043135822763672134"><b>4.5 Stars!</b><br/><br/>This book collected so much dust on my kindle shelf it's not even funny. <br/><br/>Yeah....just call me an <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431613248ra/14853567.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>...because this book was good. Really good. <br/><br/>Now, I have some minor complaints. It was a bit long. 9700+ loc...yeah <b>#lengthaversion </b> <br/><br/>And the sex was about 3 steps up from fade to black. Not descriptive and detailed at all. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431613248ra/14853568.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>But damn, I loved this one anyways.<br/><br/>D...<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1430706517ra/14750669.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>D was quiet and moody and closed off. But when he wasn't, he was so sweet.<br/><br/>I wish he would have talked "normal" but I got over that. </span>
  <span id="freeText3043135822763672134" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Stars!</b><br><br>This book collected so much dust on my kindle shelf it's not even funny. <br><br>Yeah....just call me an <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431613248ra/14853567.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>...because this book was good. Really good. <br><br>Now, I have some minor complaints. It was a bit long. 9700+ loc...yeah <b>#lengthaversion </b> <br><br>And the sex was about 3 steps up from fade to black. Not descriptive and detailed at all. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431613248ra/14853568.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But damn, I loved this one anyways.<br><br>D...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1430706517ra/14750669.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>D was quiet and moody and closed off. But when he wasn't, he was so sweet.<br><br>I wish he would have talked "normal" but I got over that. <br><br>Despite the length, I was never bored. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394261552ra/8829501.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There were plenty of edge of your seat moments. But the pace was slow, slower than I prefer...which made for a nice slow burn though between D and Jack. <br><br>The story was great. The characters were great. <br><br>I think a "sequel" has been in the works? Is still in the works? I don't know...since this one was released in 2009. But I would definitely read more from this author. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431613248i/14853570.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<tr class="no_border feedFooterReview" id="update_comment_stuff_Review757688517">

<div id="review_532048327" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/532048327" />
    <a title="Ingie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15589375-ingie"><img alt="Ingie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1477339772p2/15589375.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/532048327?book_show_action=true">Feb 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ingie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ingie" href="/user/show/15589375-ingie">Ingie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/21938408-zero-at-the-bone">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15589375-ingie?shelf=books-i-read-2013">books-i-read-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15589375-ingie?shelf=c-amazing-5-stars-2013">c-amazing-5-stars-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15589375-ingie?shelf=books-i-read-2015">books-i-read-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15589375-ingie?shelf=romance-m-m-novels">romance-m-m-novels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15589375-ingie?shelf=c-amazing-5-stars-2015">c-amazing-5-stars-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15589375-ingie?shelf=romance-m-m-audio">romance-m-m-audio</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer532048327" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11902258079390973604"><i>Written January 8, 2015</i><br/><br/><b>Re-reading - ...this time listening to the 13:20 hrs audiobook narrated by <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/8474436.Alan_Smith' title='Alan Smith' rel='nofollow noopener'>Alan Smith</a>.</b><br/><br/>This was one of my first M/M romances back in May 2013 and I loved it. Soooo very much. Still loving it? <br/><br/><a href='http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Stars/imagejpg1_zps79ce5941.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420658718i/13248486.jpg' alt=' photo imagejpg1_zps79ce5941.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>YAY!! ...still 5 big stars</b> <br/>I'm glad I read it first but the audiobook was a fun way to meet these amazing lovebirds and enjoy this thrilling storyplot once again. I feel I missed a bit of D's way of funny talking here but all in all okay done by this narrator and not a boring minut</span>
  <span id="freeText11902258079390973604" style="display:none"><i>Written January 8, 2015</i><br><br><b>Re-reading - ...this time listening to the 13:20 hrs audiobook narrated by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/8474436.Alan_Smith" title="Alan Smith" rel="nofollow noopener">Alan Smith</a>.</b><br><br>This was one of my first M/M romances back in May 2013 and I loved it. Soooo very much. Still loving it? <br><br><a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Stars/imagejpg1_zps79ce5941.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420658718i/13248486.jpg" alt=" photo imagejpg1_zps79ce5941.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>YAY!! ...still 5 big stars</b> <br>I'm glad I read it first but the audiobook was a fun way to meet these amazing lovebirds and enjoy this thrilling storyplot once again. I feel I missed a bit of D's way of funny talking here but all in all okay done by this narrator and not a boring minute.<br><br>As I said to a friend: <i>“It was a good audiobook. I enjoyed these 13 listening hours and I might do it once more in the future, this is maybe my all time favorite M/M book.”</i><br><br><br><b>**********************************************<br><br>My original review:</b> <br><br>(I first read <i>Zero at the Bone</i>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2892465.Jane_Seville" title="Jane Seville" rel="nofollow noopener">Jane Seville</a>'s only, but amazing enjoying, suspense romance 8-10 May, 2013. I dare not read what I wrote then but I guess it still applies.)<br><br><b>**********************************************</b><br><br><a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Stars/imagejpg1_zps79ce5941.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420658718i/13248486.jpg" alt=" photo imagejpg1_zps79ce5941.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>Written May 11, 2013</i><br><br><b>5 Huge Stars - A great lovestory and a thrilling escape &amp; hunt plot for an eternal happiness end</b><br><br><b>The surgeon Jack Francisco</b> becomes a witness to a mob murder and is put into protective custody until he can testify. <br><br><b>A hitman known as just "D"</b> becomes forced a contract to kill the blueeyed doctor. According to D's own code of whom he takes elimination contracts on, he instead, takes Jack on a run. D sees as his task to ensure that Jack will be able to testify in the trial. <br><br><b>An action loaded escape begins...</b><br><blockquote>"Pizza's good"<br>Francisco sat up, frowning. "Oh, you want some?"<br>"I'm hungry too." D watched Francisco's bemused expression. "What?"<br>Francisco shrugged, shaking it off. "I don't know. It's just weird that you, you know... eat."</blockquote><br><b>When I started reading this novel</b>, I thought I'd got an suspense story with some pieces of added nice M/M romance stuff. But o'boy how wrong I was. I had instead received a grand, tenderly told, love story about two very different men. Two men from completely different worlds, with different backgrounds, experiences and life situations. <br><br># <b>Jack is easygoing</b>, think well of others and cares about right and wrong. He is successful at work but a little lonely. Setting up as a witness against the Mafia, he wants to do it, although it will change his whole future and life. <br><br># <b>D however, has lived in the shadows</b> for so long that he doesn't allow himself any feelings or kind of normal life anymore. He is one of the best in his field, but have since long lost every hope for himself. He has no friends or any human contact with others outside the "job".<blockquote>
  <a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Love/324475194_cca50e7d7d_o_zps76e5f3a6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409029i/800626.jpg" alt=" photo 324475194_cca50e7d7d_o_zps76e5f3a6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</blockquote><br><b>What's so nice</b> is that Jack immediately rely on D - D is his lifeline and savior against the danger. The story tells us step by step, how the this two approaches and find one another. They are both strong and emotional men, but find it really hard and difficult to dress their feelings in words for starts. It leave actions and gestures to show the way. And it does, they are both willing to risk everthing for each other. <br><br><b>These guys are two wonderful and easily loved characters</b>. Two so different characters, but they are now both deep inside my <i>book-boy-heart</i> for a very long time.<br><blockquote>
<a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Pics/cherries_051_crop_zpsf29b26d9.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409029i/800627.jpg" alt=" photo cherries_051_crop_zpsf29b26d9.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>..."I'd bite of one side a the shell real careful-like, so non a the syrup spilled, then suck all the gooey out, then fish out the cherry with my tounge, then I'd just have the chocolate shell left and I'd nibble on it 'til it was gone."...</blockquote><br><b>There is so much happening</b> in this story and I will not even try to share a single percent of everything. You just read it! To say, however, is that this is a book about two men who find their true love. It's about their hardships to achieve the new love and in the background is a really exciting action-story going on. You get some nail bits scenes and a thrilling persistent anxiety until the end. The death threats are there all the time and I wondered nervously how it could work out and be a wonderful HEA at the end. <b>But don't worry it IS a true romance</b> - you get what you want - a nicely finished LOVE story.<br><br><b>Any heat and steam?</b> Yes, described in the finest way, tenderly and lovingly. <br><blockquote>
  <a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Love/gay_zpsad987a63.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409029i/800628.jpg" alt=" photo gay_zpsad987a63.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</blockquote><br><b>An added plus</b> for the superb finish with a long and glorious epilogue. Among the better ones I've read in a long time. It provides, as this novel in general, a lull in the narration of the events. I could feel each scene, know what D and Jack felt and had time to enjoy the wonderful sweet dialogue. Did I mention D's dialect? [tough at first for a girl who learned English in school] It is absolutely a great fun to read D's "voice" and it gave me so much more to his character. <blockquote>"What would it have been like?" Jack whispered. Lying on their sides, face to face, just staring at each other for what felt like hours, drifting off and waking again.<br>D sighed, tucked his hand underneath his head. "Maybe...get a house. Never had no house a my own."<br>"With a garden."<br>"Yeah, so's you could come inside smellin' like sunshine after weddin."</blockquote><br>A great, hot and thrilling read. Sweet and lovely D &amp; Jack - <br><i>Love it, love that, love them...</i><br><br><b>I LIKE - Enormously good, I'm more than satisfied.</b><br><br><br>*****<br><i>Don't miss to read three nice shorties with small glimpses of Jack and D's daily life after the novel ended <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11196941.Date_Night__Zero_at_the_Bone___1_1_" title="Date Night (Zero at the Bone, #1.1) by Jane Seville" rel="nofollow noopener">Date Night</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11196920.Time_After_Time__Zero_at_the_Bone___1_2_" title="Time After Time (Zero at the Bone, #1.2) by Jane Seville" rel="nofollow noopener">Time After Time</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11324929.Liar__Zero_at_the_Bone___1_3_" title="Liar (Zero at the Bone, #1.3) by Jane Seville" rel="nofollow noopener">Liar</a> (ten pages each - available for free to download). <br><br>There is also a Christmas story and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9994651.A_Very_D_Christmas__Zero_at_the_Bone___1_4_" title="A Very D Christmas (Zero at the Bone, #1.4) by Jane Seville" rel="nofollow noopener">A Very D Christmas</a> (some fifty pages - to buy).</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="11902258079390973604" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Pavlina Read more sleep less blog❤❤  " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6603203-pavlina-read-more-sleep-less-blog"><img alt="Pavlina Read more sleep less blog❤❤  " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1596881564p2/6603203.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/607443198?book_show_action=true">May 05, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pavlina Read more sleep less blog❤❤  " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pavlina Read more sleep less blog❤❤  " href="/user/show/6603203-pavlina-read-more-sleep-less-blog">Pavlina Read more sleep less blog❤❤  </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer607443198" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17021417322586089875"><b>Buddy reading with Melissa <3 <3</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420378i/833896.jpg' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The plot it was amazing!!I highly recommend this story for those who enjoy thrillers and romantic suspense while appreciating a slow build romance.<br/><br/>Zero at the Bone is about a surgeon(Jack) whose life is in peril when he becomes a witness to a mob hit..D is an assassin and he can choose and what he doesn't want to do..But this time he can't refuse,he is blackmailed into killing Jack.When D meets Jack, he really isn't able to kill the man,the innocence of the man is</span>
  <span id="freeText17021417322586089875" style="display:none"><b>Buddy reading with Melissa &lt;3 &lt;3</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420378i/833896.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The plot it was amazing!!I highly recommend this story for those who enjoy thrillers and romantic suspense while appreciating a slow build romance.<br><br>Zero at the Bone is about a surgeon(Jack) whose life is in peril when he becomes a witness to a mob hit..D is an assassin and he can choose and what he doesn't want to do..But this time he can't refuse,he is blackmailed into killing Jack.When D meets Jack, he really isn't able to kill the man,the innocence of the man is clear in his eyes and D is tired to let people die due to an event that isn't their fault. <br>So they go on the run and are forced to work together to keep unknown forces from killing them both.Not knowing who to trust or where to turn except to each other...<br><br>The relationship between Jack and D is intense and emotional.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420378i/833897.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420378i/833898.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>Jack definitely is the more expressive type and his personality fits with why he doesn’t let things drop with D.He’s curious and honest.The last fact makes for amusing moments when he finally admits his attraction to D and what will happen from there on.His devotion to D!! He starting worries over why he allowed himself and D to develop a relationship. <br><br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420378i/833899.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>D is yummy with a sexy accent assasin!!His blunt nature especially with Jack is a great set up for laughs and smiles.I apreciate how layered he was!!D turns from enemy to protector and he appoints himself the only protector of Jack...<br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420378i/833900.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>The ending was what I wanted for Jack &amp; D!!Setting up home,loving and caring for each other and having a happy life together. <br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420378i/833901._SY540_.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>For more reviews you can check mine and Kristinas's blog. :D<br><br> <a href="http://readmore-sleepless.blogspot.gr/" rel="nofollow noopener">my link text</a><br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380387651i/747742.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> </span>

<div id="review_3491623148" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3491623148" />
    <a title="Princess under cover" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9604542-princess-under-cover"><img alt="Princess under cover" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1541254101p2/9604542.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3491623148?book_show_action=true">Aug 11, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Princess under cover" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Princess under cover" href="/user/show/9604542-princess-under-cover">Princess under cover</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3491623148" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10758061923686974111">Alright folks, what can I say? I loved this one. With a few caveats:<br/><br/><b>1) You have to suspend belief.</b> Just leave all credibility at the door and come inside this crazy unbelievable story. Go along for the ride.<br/><br/><b>2) Ignore the lack of editing. </b>Just forget everything that pisses you off about typos and grammar and all of that. Forget it. Let it slide off you like water off a duck's feathers.<br/><br/><b>3) Never mind about a smooth, perfect flow</b>, just the right pace with the right things happening at the right time</span>
  <span id="freeText10758061923686974111" style="display:none">Alright folks, what can I say? I loved this one. With a few caveats:<br><br><b>1) You have to suspend belief.</b> Just leave all credibility at the door and come inside this crazy unbelievable story. Go along for the ride.<br><br><b>2) Ignore the lack of editing. </b>Just forget everything that pisses you off about typos and grammar and all of that. Forget it. Let it slide off you like water off a duck's feathers.<br><br><b>3) Never mind about a smooth, perfect flow</b>, just the right pace with the right things happening at the right time. And don't look beyond the last paragraph looking for maybe a few more pages thinking - huh? it ended right THERE?? Weird...<br><br><b>4) Don't be annoyed that sometimes without warning POVs shift</b>, and even from 3rd person past POV to first person present POV, just don't be bothered by it. Pfft, let it roll... <br><br><b>NOW. You're ready to enjoy this ULTRA-EXPENSIVE, un-professionally proofed (as in, was it proofed at all???) book. Which has golden nuggets of memorable writing on almost every page amidst the rough edges :)</b><br><br><b>As you see below, I love D. Just love him to pieces.</b> He carried the whole story for me. And look, I had a couple moments of admiration for Jack, and I kinda get why D falls for him, but that was about it. Jack is more "normal" shall we say - he has all kinds of doubts, normal emotional responses to situations and I didn't like the fact that he was still doubting his relationship with D after everything D has done for him while they were separated toward the end, but on the other hand, it's understandable. <br><br><b>Now D-- Lord, he ticks all my boxes for fave type of Hero:<br><br>(BTW, he's blond, and if he let his hair grow, it would be curly blond... I struggled to find the perfect images for him, but here are some):<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1597425455i/29967602.png" width="402" height="494" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>A little too hairy, it's true, but like the gruffy macho man-ness of it all :P<br><br>* Man's man<br><br>* Man of few words, but feels soooooo deeply<br><br>* Total opposite of man-whore - the guy was celibate for 10+ years!!! Not since his ex-wife! And several years since he even jerked off! Like WHAT?? Pretty much a virgin. And it was a PLEASURE in so many ways to see him come alive<br><br>* Total badass- like how he tags on the implicit and explicit "dumbass" at the end of most sentences :P<br><br>* Once he loves, that's IT. Nothing else for him. Literally. If Jack died, he was going to off himself, and if he lived, he was never going to have sex again. Given his lack of activity and interest for 10+ years!! I believe him. And if that seems totally abnormal to some ppl, what did I tell you about suspending belief? I happen to LOVE it.</b><br><br>So the story went like this:<br><br>*Jack witnessed a murder that got him some really powerful enemies and D is an assassin blackmailed to do him. Except D has a conscience<br><br>* I liked best the first 1/3 when they're getting to know each other despite D's reticence. Jack's persistent and unafraid. Was doing a double-take when they suddenly started thinking about their "feelings" for each other and I was like - WHAT? What did I miss? I missed nothing. This is one of those sudden things you gotta get over in this book<br><br>* Then, there's like 1/3 of nonstop sex. Which I didn't mind AT ALL. But sorta disorienting in the middle of an action/ assassin/ killers after you book. Suddenly turned into erotica. Oh and suspend all belief about protection and lube bc first time they did it - there was neither. And oh! It just went right in with a bit of pain. Done. <b>SUSPEND ALL BELIEF PPL!! </b>And every time since the first time, no condom in sight. So......<br><br>* Anywho, then we get into the action again and suddenly secret friends of D's are coming out of the woodwork - like this whole X thing that I was like, OK, where are we planning to go with this - set up for next novel? Where is the next novel BTW?? Weird.<br><br>* Then some more sex sprinkled in there, then not much of a final "climax" to the whole situation, sort of main conflict just went away <br><br>* Then it was epilogue of how an ex-assassin was living life with a surgeon, D struggling with a particularly bad case and thinking about marrying Jack and... <br><br>THE END.<br><br>Eh????<br><br>Well, it was entertaining, and like I said I enjoyed D to the max, so... what the hay, 5 stars.<br><br><br><br><br>5% in , I do not regret forking over $10. Worth it already.<br><br>Here's D, except with hair...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1597202114ra/29951632.gif" width="593" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Maybe this is D, but retaining Jason Statham's bad-assed-ness.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1597202114i/29951635.jpg" width="236" height="360" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Or this:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1597202114i/29951633.jpg" width="236" height="325" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Annnnnndddd, back to Jason:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1597202114i/29951634._SY540_.png" width="500" height="731" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="10758061923686974111" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_112112076" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/112112076" />
    <a title="Mel" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2295424-mel"><img alt="Mel" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1305638929p2/2295424.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/112112076?book_show_action=true">Jul 17, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mel" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mel" href="/user/show/2295424-mel">Mel</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2295424-mel?shelf=m-m">m-m</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2295424-mel?shelf=e-book">e-book</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer112112076" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1989096384450126137">Warning: I’m not going to make friends with this review. In fact: I might lose some, ha! But <i>Zero at the Bone</i> -practically considered a classic in the m/m genre- didn't do it for me. Most I can make of it is: ‘meh’, which translates to 2,5 stars. <br/><br/>It started out well: I really liked the premise of the story, I liked the fact that Jack held his own despite being helpless in the situation and I was intrigued by the dark and brooding D. I loved D's internal monologue about his vault, in which he kep</span>
  <span id="freeText1989096384450126137" style="display:none">Warning: I’m not going to make friends with this review. In fact: I might lose some, ha! But <i>Zero at the Bone</i> -practically considered a classic in the m/m genre- didn't do it for me. Most I can make of it is: ‘meh’, which translates to 2,5 stars. <br /><br />It started out well: I really liked the premise of the story, I liked the fact that Jack held his own despite being helpless in the situation and I was intrigued by the dark and brooding D. I loved D's internal monologue about his vault, in which he kept his dark secrets hidden from the world, and I really liked the way the men interacted... Basically: I was pretty much satisfied until around 40% in.<br /><br />Sadly: as the story progressed, the plot became more silly, the characters more annoying (Jack) and flat (D) and the whole thing just got too sappy for my taste. <br />Jack turned into a damsel in distress. And I don't use the term 'damsel' loosely: he became a girl. His level of passive aggressiveness rivaled that of many (annoying) PNR heroine. On top of that, he kept wanting to <i>talk</i>. And when I mean 'talk' I mean: pressuring D for his inner most thoughts -to the point of coming across as inconsiderate and demanding. <br />And as for D: his short sentences and his aggravating accent (does anyone actually talk like that?) got on my nerves after a while. He seemed like a caricature, the archetype of the brooding, dangerous mystery man. Intriguing initially, but silly after a while. <br /><br />The plot was far fetched but made some sense until about halfway into the book. Ending the story there (and leaving it semi open) would have been a better idea, I would have given it a 4 star rating at that point. But no: the book just went on and on and on. And with that, the story lost its pace, excitement and most of all: credibility. It became a weird mixture of bad action movie meets bad soap opera. <br />The main plot about the bad guy following D didn't make any sense at all. Besides: I was surprised by the fact that all supposed professionals turned incompetent and the amateur Jack suddenly had professional skills. I also didn't get how our guys changed from grown men to two adolescent girls, to the point of getting into some PDA while they had a gun to their heads. Also: (minor detail but no less annoying) what was up with sex in the beginning? No lube, no preparation? Really? <br />And to top off all this silliness: there was a huge dose of sap. And I hate sap.<br /><br />So, all in all: Zero at the Bone was a huge let down for me. I'm sure it's enjoyable for some, but if you're one for a more realistic and nuanced approach and you're not a big fan of sap, skip this. </span>
  <a data-text-id="1989096384450126137" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_72218202" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/72218202" />
    <a title="Lily" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2343400-lily"><img alt="Lily" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1314930144p2/2343400.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/72218202?book_show_action=true">Sep 23, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lily" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lily" href="/user/show/2343400-lily">Lily</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2343400-lily?shelf=what-i-read-in-2009">what-i-read-in-2009</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2343400-lily?shelf=cops-pi-bodyguards">cops-pi-bodyguards</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2343400-lily?shelf=m-m">m-m</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2343400-lily?shelf=loved-it">loved-it</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2343400-lily?shelf=action-mystery-suspense">action-mystery-suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2343400-lily?shelf=length-novel">length-novel</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2343400-lily?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2343400-lily?shelf=ebook">ebook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2343400-lily?shelf=medical">medical</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2343400-lily?shelf=challenge-books-2009">challenge-books-2009</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer72218202" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16071575518655901485">Read again for the <i>Re-Romancing Favorites Challenge</i> and I loved it just as much as the first time I read it.<br/><br/><br/>Original review from Nov 2009:<br/>Dr. Jack Francisco witnesses a murder as he leaves work one day and before he knows it his life has changed completely. Taken into protective custody and moved across country until he can testify against the killers, Jack finds himself separated from his friends, family and patients. While he is naturally upset at the situation Jack is at heart a good and hono</span>
  <span id="freeText16071575518655901485" style="display:none">Read again for the <i>Re-Romancing Favorites Challenge</i> and I loved it just as much as the first time I read it.<br /><br /><br />Original review from Nov 2009:<br />Dr. Jack Francisco witnesses a murder as he leaves work one day and before he knows it his life has changed completely. Taken into protective custody and moved across country until he can testify against the killers, Jack finds himself separated from his friends, family and patients. While he is naturally upset at the situation Jack is at heart a good and honorable man and knows that he needs to do everything he can to bring the killers to justice.<br /><br />D is a hit man with a conscience. An apparent cold and ruthless killer he nevertheless draws the line at killing innocent "good" people. When his handler brings him the contract to kill a witness to a murder he turns it down. Unfortunately for D someone is determined to make him take the job. Blackmailed but with no clue as to who is forcing him D accepts the contract to kill Jack Francisco. But when he's face to face with his intended victim D can't kill him. He recognizes that Jack is a good man and instead of killing him D knows he must protect Jack from the other hit men who are sure to accept the contract that he isn't fulfilling.<br /><br />What follows is an action packed thriller that is full of suspense and action yet at the same time is also an emotional and sensual story. These two men are total opposites yet develop a connection that profoundly affects their lives. I really loved both Jack and D. Jack is outgoing, secure in who he is, looks for the good in others and I found his personality to be a good foil for D's quiet and taciturn nature. For all that D is a killer and appears to be totally unemotional he is in fact a man who has suffered so much and done things he's sure he can never be forgiven for. Full of guilt for a tragedy he blames himself for he has closed himself off from his emotions.<br /><br />On the run from the people that are after them both they find themselves drawn more and more to each other. Jack is able to slowly get D to open up and start to accept that he is in fact not just the killer he judges himself to be but rather a man who has seen and done both good and bad in his life. I absolutely loved the way the relationship between them develops from their first meeting where D holds Jack's very life in his hands to the end of the story where it's clear that they have found in each other a love that makes them complete in all ways.<br /><br />The secondary characters in this story are also very well written. From the agents helping Jack to the bad guys trying to kill him as well as D's associates, these characters all contribute in some way to the storyline. In a book this long, over 300 pages, it would be easy to populate it with 'filler' characters but in this case the flow and development of the story incorporates the secondary characters quite well.<br /><br />Another aspect that I really enjoyed was the attention to detail presented throughout the book. The ins and outs of being a hit man as well as the information on the Witness Protection program was very interesting to read. I enjoyed the adventure as D and Jack went on the run as well as the more relaxing times as they hunkered down and got to know each other. Reading the book I could so clearly see what a fabulous movie it could be. Two heroes, one noble and kind, the other a tortured soul needing to be saved, bad guys galore, lots of thrills and adventure and through it all a wonderfully emotional love story with some super hot sex scenes. I'd plunk down my money at my local movie theater to see it. And buy the DVD to watch it again and again.<br /><br />This absolutely fantastic story is intense and gripping from page one to the very end and you just won't want to put it down. The plot is fast paced yet flows really well throughout. The strength of the story however is in the characters themselves, Jack and D and the dynamics of their relationship. I loved how Jack was slowly able to get D to let him see the real man under the hit man facade and that D was able to lean on Jack and come to believe in himself once again. While there are several explicit and hot sex scenes in the book they are not in any way the main focus of the book. Instead it's the emotional bond and the trust and love that develops between these two very different men that's the focus of the book.<br /><br />Zero at the Bone is one of the most intense and satisfying stories I've read this year. Wonderfully written with great characters and a tightly woven plot this is a book that I know I'll enjoy reading many times over. Definitely 5 stars and I highly recommend it.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16071575518655901485" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
