<div id="review_591384254" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/591384254" />
    <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole"><img alt="Duchess Nicole" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1499265843p2/2204947.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/591384254?book_show_action=true">Apr 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Duchess Nicole" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole">Duchess Nicole</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Duchess Nicole by: </span>
      Baba ♥♥♥ Marcus, Tyler, Tate, Dan, Ty, &amp; Hunter
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=ebooks-i-own-not-bn">ebooks-i-own-not-bn</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=sigh-worthy">sigh-worthy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=recommendations">recommendations</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=genre-contemp-romance">genre-contemp-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=mm-romance">mm-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=stand-alone">stand-alone</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=e-pcs">e-pcs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=genre-romantic-suspense">genre-romantic-suspense</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer591384254" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2494596145224593292">First off, I've gotta say that I love this cover...rarely do I see a cover match up so exactly with what I have in my head but this D and Jack is perfect...body language and all. D is sort of badass and standoffish, Jack is a bit more boyish and nervous. I love it!!!<br/><br/>This is a story about a hit man, D, and and his mark, Jack. You'd think that no excuse is good enough to convince you that a man who kills other people for a living could be a good person, but D can change your mind. He's not ALL goo</span>
  <span id="freeText2494596145224593292" style="display:none">First off, I've gotta say that I love this cover...rarely do I see a cover match up so exactly with what I have in my head but this D and Jack is perfect...body language and all. D is sort of badass and standoffish, Jack is a bit more boyish and nervous. I love it!!!<br><br>This is a story about a hit man, D, and and his mark, Jack. You'd think that no excuse is good enough to convince you that a man who kills other people for a living could be a good person, but D can change your mind. He's not ALL good. He still kills people. But he gets to choose which jobs he takes, and he would normally pass a job like Jack up...D does have some scruples. Under threat of exposure, D is forced to put a gun to Jack's head...if only D didn't fell like he was losing his own humanity...<br><b>
  <blockquote>"He didn't like to think about how far gone he was into the abyss that even the humanness of lust was now foreign to him. At least he still felt hunger, and cold, and the craving for nicotine. How long until event hose animal sensations left him? Would he eventually be left with nothing but a set of skills that suited him for only one profession, and a head full of things he didn't want to know? Maybe he's disconnect enough that he would no longer swear, or piss, or get stupid songs stuck in his head. He's been told over and over again that he'd have to become a machine, but he hadn't really believed that he would. He knew better now."</blockquote>
</b><br><br>Jack has worked for the last decade to get to where he is now...a maxillofacial surgeon who has not one but two college degrees, his work is his life. But now life as he know it is over. He's under witness protection after witnessing a mob like hit on an innocent woman, and has been forced to give up everything he's ever known...friends, family, job, house, life...<br><br>Now they are on the run together, hiding from some really bad people...people who used to be D's bosses and colleagues...who can and are trying their hardest to find Jack and D. But D's really freaking good at hiding. Which leads to a lot of down time for these two. A lot of time to to know each other. And their romance is so slow building, growing by miniscule increments. It's easy to see how these two fall in love...and it's real love, not the kind of lust that is life affirming in the face of death. Because D is just that badass, and Jack becomes quite proficient at badassery as well...<br><br>Honestly, the best part of this book for me was watching D accept who he is...not as a gay man, but as a man. A person deserving of the love that Jack has to offer him. I just feel so bad for D. His lot in life has been one of pure hell, all of it not under his own control. Circumstances have led him again and again into tragedy, and it's no wonder that he's shut down his emotions to the extent that he has. The way that Jack is able to get inside him is what fairy tales are made of if they're not made up by Disney. This dawning realization that Jack could very well be his soul mate...it's breathtaking.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417782i/826670.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <blockquote>
<i>"To think I almos' put a bullet between them eyes, and took that life that now I'd die ta save, and I never woulda known what he was in the world, and who he was or could be, and I woulda never even known what I was misin', nor known how right it could feel just ta lay my fingers alongside his.</i>"</blockquote>
</b><br><br>The sex is fairly PG13 for the most part...I'd not call this erotic at all. It's more romance than anything. It's a story of two people from such opposite walks of life who are thrown into circumstances that almost seem serendipitous. D and Jack are just meant to be together. They heal each other, they soothe each other, and this is their story...Oh, and the epilogue!!!! Made me so happy...all is not automatically bright and shiny for these two. But you do know how much they love each other, and you can feel how content they are.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417782ra/826671.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="2494596145224593292" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_226390110" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/226390110" />
    <a title="Nile Princess" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6203427-nile-princess"><img alt="Nile Princess" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1386342613p2/6203427.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/226390110?book_show_action=true">Oct 22, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nile Princess" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nile Princess" href="/user/show/6203427-nile-princess">Nile Princess</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/6393872-zero-at-the-bone">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6203427-nile-princess?shelf=m-m-romance">m-m-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6203427-nile-princess?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6203427-nile-princess?shelf=couldn-t-finish">couldn-t-finish</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6203427-nile-princess?shelf=special-ops-military">special-ops-military</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6203427-nile-princess?shelf=assassins">assassins</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6203427-nile-princess?shelf=it-must-be-me">it-must-be-me</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer226390110" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6115086769786993941">Maybe it's that I'm getting more demanding or impatient, or no longer feel the need to suffer through books that aren't holding my interest, but at 35% I just gave up. I had high hopes for this one. There were lots of great reviews and I really liked the premise, but the actual delivery fell short.<br/><br/>Jack, a surgeon, witnesses a murder and agrees to testify. He's taken into protective custody. D, an assassin, takes the job to take him out. Everything was going well, right up until the moment these </span>
  <span id="freeText6115086769786993941" style="display:none">Maybe it's that I'm getting more demanding or impatient, or no longer feel the need to suffer through books that aren't holding my interest, but at 35% I just gave up. I had high hopes for this one. There were lots of great reviews and I really liked the premise, but the actual delivery fell short.<br /><br />Jack, a surgeon, witnesses a murder and agrees to testify. He's taken into protective custody. D, an assassin, takes the job to take him out. Everything was going well, right up until the moment these two actually meet. I like the author's writing style; she actually made me laugh out loud a few times but the pacing on this just didn't work for me. D is a hardened shell of a man who only lives to kill, so to have him go from that to a guy talking about feelings and wanting to give up his life for Jack needed a slow, firm hand guided by nuance and subtlety. What we got was hokey sappiness. D's journey was not given its due. The dialogue was groan worthy. Don't have D tell us, about a third of the way in, that he feels like he's been dead inside and now he feels alive (rolls eyes), show us!! I couldn't even see a hardened assassin saying some of the stuff that came out of his mouth. I did enjoy Jack taking care of him while he was hurt, but that brings us to the other problem.<br /><br />Why was D so inept?? If he's supposed to be one of the best out there, then the mercenary world is truly in shambles. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[He gets shot days after meeting Jack, and manages to have Jack kidnapped out from right under his nose. Really? He stays in the same place for days, doesn't do perimeter checks or install extra security. Instead, they're out shopping for groceries in the local town and playing chess like they're on vacation. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Jack was, by turns, sassily cute and naive and annoying. You don't have someone shake a lifetime of mistrust in days by asking them a million questions and forcing them to talk to you. And what was up with his self-lubricating orifice? First time sex with no lube whatsoever and no difficulty being penetrated AND he was able to come seconds later without D touching his penis at all. Gay men everywhere should be so lucky.<br /><br />I realize that there are lots of people who liked this book, but I can't recommend it with any seriousness.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6115086769786993941" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

Feel free to tell me I 've been stupid.<br/><br/>First of all, D is Jason Statham. He is, it's not just me, right?   <span id="freeText12282035950384510582" style="display:none"><b>*4.5 stars*</b><br><br>Why did I wait so long to read this book??? Why? Feel free to tell me I 've been stupid.<br><br>First of all, D is Jason Statham. He is, it's not just me, right? Seriously, look!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440249935i/15952295.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440249935i/15952296.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What can I say that hasn't already been said?<br><br>Very long book, but I never got bored, not for one second. <b>Fast paced, with a surprise around every corner, this is probably the BEST romantic suspence I 've ever read.</b><br><br>The dual POV that changed quite often worked great, and<b> when we sometimes got the POV of some secondary characters, it was really needed.</b><br><br>I loved how the hard core hitman took one look at Jack and knew he wouldn't kill him...<br><br><i>
  <b>"Biggest damned eyes I ever saw on any man, and bluer’n the sky down in Bryce Canyon. Big enough ta hold all the life in him so’s I can see it, the life they want me ta take, the life I’ll hafta stand here and watch leave him."</b>
</i><br><br>I loved how falling in love with Jack, made D come alive and change...<br><br><i>
  <b> “You thought if you could keep the dark away from me, that maybe some of it would leave you too.”<br>............................<br>“Thanks for my life.”<br> “Thanks for mine.”</b>
</i><br><br>I loved the sexy times, the times when they had to leave each other, the funny moments, the chocolate-covered cherries...I loved every single thing.<br><br>The only reason I removed half a star is because I wanted a little more background on Jack. He says he's gay, doesn't mention any previous relatonship to a man but he 's been married to a woman. It confused me a little but it didn't really bother me.<br><br>If there is someone out there who hasn't read this, do it now!<br><br>Where is this author? Doesn't she write anymore? Now that I 've found her!<br><br></span>

  <span id="freeText7318970993971089357" style="display:none">This was great. I dip into M/M now and again. It is not my usual reading genre. Loved this one. Really good story - kept me guessing all the time. Jack was great but D. was yummy. Only complaint was they way he talked - just got on my nerves a bit but eventually got used to it. It was sort of left open that there could be a sequel as D. is still on a Case ..... would be nice to see how they are getting on further down the line. Think I might be off to catch me a Highlander now.</span>

<div id="review_513199593" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/513199593" />
    <a title="Macky" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7500424-macky"><img alt="Macky" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1548352117p2/7500424.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/513199593?book_show_action=true">Jan 21, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7500424-macky?shelf=all-time-favourite">all-time-favourite</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7500424-macky?shelf=own">own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7500424-macky?shelf=lgbt">lgbt</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer513199593" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12471087852191775546">I love it when authors do a ' mix up ' and veer away from the expected. Jane Seville takes an anti hero assassin like D and pairs him with ' Mr normal ' Jack who is in the wrong place at the wrong time and weaves one of the best gay fiction stories around them that I think I will ever read. This book has everything - a proper gutsy, gritty crime backstory that never loses pace or excitement ( edge of the seat stuff ) and one of the best m/ m romances in the genre that starts slowly and ends up p</span>
  <span id="freeText12471087852191775546" style="display:none">I love it when authors do a ' mix up ' and veer away from the expected. Jane Seville takes an anti hero assassin like D and pairs him with ' Mr normal ' Jack who is in the wrong place at the wrong time and weaves one of the best gay fiction stories around them that I think I will ever read. This book has everything - a proper gutsy, gritty crime backstory that never loses pace or excitement ( edge of the seat stuff ) and one of the best m/ m romances in the genre that starts slowly and ends up packing a real emotional punch. The list of adjectives to describe this story are endless as it has lots of different layers to it. Exciting, sexy, tender, poignant, witty, funny, sensual, surprising.......... and perfectly balanced love scenes ,in amount and description. Bliss!<br /><br />The love that grows between the MC's makes this book the success it is and for me is the true heart of the novel. It was a privilege to be on the outskirts watching it unfold and it will NEVER leave my Kindle library. I first read this a couple of years ago and constantly watch out to see if Jane Seville has produced anything else, but as yet no joy, so for now I'll just have to keep coming back to Jack and D for my fix - No hardship!<br /><br /><b> EDITED 14/11/13 </b> <br /><br />Just finished reading this for the second time and don't need to alter my original review but just want to add that I didn't think it possible to enjoy this any more than I did the first time round, but holy hell that was an amazing reread! Buddy read it with my awesome girlies Tina and Gina and had a blast! Thanks my loves. If I could quadruple the rating on this I would.. Jack &amp; D you are in my heart forever! <br /><br />What a love story... I go gooey just thinking about it. Slow burning but passionate and so exciting.. Anything that could be picked at just goes right out of the window because of the way it grabs my heartstrings and engages my emotions. An all time favourite with two of my most loved men. Delightful, delicious and sublime! One can only hope that one day they come back and let us into their lives again... I keep wishing! </span>
  <a data-text-id="12471087852191775546" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_2664659874" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2664659874" />
    <a title="Gerbera_Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/68687480-gerbera-reads"><img alt="Gerbera_Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1578061403p2/68687480.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2664659874?book_show_action=true">Jul 29, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Gerbera_Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Gerbera_Reads" href="/user/show/68687480-gerbera-reads">Gerbera_Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/6393872-zero-at-the-bone">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/68687480-gerbera-reads?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/68687480-gerbera-reads?shelf=mystery">mystery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/68687480-gerbera-reads?shelf=crime">crime</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/68687480-gerbera-reads?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/68687480-gerbera-reads?shelf=suspense">suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/68687480-gerbera-reads?shelf=awesome">awesome</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/68687480-gerbera-reads?shelf=great-read">great-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/68687480-gerbera-reads?shelf=must-read">must-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/68687480-gerbera-reads?shelf=nemesis">nemesis</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2664659874" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12835349951643156622">This was one fine book. I loved the action, the suspense and the way Ms Seville chose to tell the story, but I absolutely adored the main characters - Jack and D. The juxtaposition of Jack's unreserved honesty and D's guarded reserve appealed greatly to me. I really liked the side characters and the mystery of X, D's friend, and their remote yet at the same time close relationship. Told from multiple POVs, the story depicts immeasurable pain, boundless courage and undying love between two men wh</span>
  <span id="freeText12835349951643156622" style="display:none">This was one fine book. I loved the action, the suspense and the way Ms Seville chose to tell the story, but I absolutely adored the main characters - Jack and D. The juxtaposition of Jack's unreserved honesty and D's guarded reserve appealed greatly to me. I really liked the side characters and the mystery of X, D's friend, and their remote yet at the same time close relationship. Told from multiple POVs, the story depicts immeasurable pain, boundless courage and undying love between two men who despite their differences found common ground and dared to reach for the impossible.<br /><br />Jack Francisco's life was ordinary - respected colleague, good-looking man and possibly a good friend. But all of that was snatched away when he unwittingly became the only witness to a murder. And after choosing to stand up and testify, his life was no longer his own. So, when he looked into a barrel of a hired gun, he thought it was over. Not quite yet! Call it Fate or not, but in the next moment he found himself on the run with the man who was supposed to kill him. Who knew that that which didn't kill him, would become the love of his life. I loved Jack's patience, his faith in D and his unfailing belief that D is deserving of love, happiness and bright future despite his past. His care of D till the very end made me admire him even more. And his testimony on the stand was the s*exiest thing ever!!!! <br /><br />D is stone cold assassin. He fears that one day he will simply cease to exist, since it's hard to feel anything at all. But despite all those that he killed, he lives by a certain code of his own - never kill an innocent. So when he is blackmailed into eliminating the witness who couldn't be any cleaner, he simply can not do it. Thus starts their trip to outrun the killers, assassins, traitors and bullets. D lost faith in human kindness, closed himself off completely, and yet here he was - a man willing to be there for him without expecting anything in return. The shift between them was so subtle, and D's shell started to crack. <br /><br />Both men open up to each other either due to forced proximity or simply because it's time. Jack is there to help D purge the poison that is slowly eroding him from inside, he is there to help D find himself again and give him something worth fighting for. From awkward moments to the most intense intimacy known to me, both D and Jack choose each other and fight for their future no matter how long or short it might be. Some moments were truly heart-warming, some almost made me cry. D has changed so much. After all he has been through, his capacity to love and cherish really amazed me. And while Jack hasn't suffered any great downfalls in his life, his courage and devotion to D and his willingness to sacrifice himself was truly admirable. <br /><br />The story was truly suspenseful even during quiet moments - it was in the air just hovering over them. From one emotional high to another, this book kept me on the edge of my seat. I loved Jack's time alone when he tried to determine what it was he felt for D. I loved D's dedication to making sure they both have a future they want. And I loved when D became Anson again. The epilogue was absolutely marvelous. I can't find enough words to express how much I love these men, the journey they've had and the happy future they have yet to live! Highly recommend it! Amazing book!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="12835349951643156622" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer5848363756317263877">MM-mystery-romance; this is the hole I've dug myself into, and I'm staying there, especially when there are stories as awesome as this one!<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1476863582ra/20889044.gif' width='' height='' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>This book has been popping up, on and off, for quite some time, but for some reason the blurb didn't get my motor running, and boy am I sorry that I haven't picked it up before now!<br/>This story was well-written, it had AWESOME, fleshed-out characters and an action-mystery that kept my attention.<br/><br/>So D is a hitman with a conscience, of sorts. His handler Josy gets</span>
  <span id="freeText5848363756317263877" style="display:none">MM-mystery-romance; this is the hole I've dug myself into, and I'm staying there, especially when there are stories as awesome as this one!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1476863582ra/20889044.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>This book has been popping up, on and off, for quite some time, but for some reason the blurb didn't get my motor running, and boy am I sorry that I haven't picked it up before now!<br>This story was well-written, it had AWESOME, fleshed-out characters and an action-mystery that kept my attention.<br><br>So D is a hitman with a conscience, of sorts. His handler Josy gets the 'job-offers' and then D decides whether the target is a 'bad enough' person for him to pay a visit. (He has his own moral compass on who deserves to die.)<br>Jack is a 'head-doctor' (not brain or feelings, but the skull and such, I could not even pronounce his title, let alone spell it) and one day when he is leaving work, he witnesses a murder by some men from a <i>Familia</i>.<br>Jack is one of the coolest characters I've read in a long time. He has grit, personality and a great moral compass; he's a GOOD guy, who is also smart. In his mind there is no question whether he will testify or not.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1476863582ra/20889045.gif" width="400" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>D is blackmailed into paying Jack a 'visit', and even though Jack is in Witsec, 'they' have his new address, and sends D there.<br>D really doesn't want to kill an 'innocent' victim, and when he meets Jack, he cannot go through with it. <br>Since other hitmen can be next in line for the 'job', and since there is something fishy with the whole situation (both for Jack AND D), D decides to help Jack and keep him safe until the trial.<br><br>What follows is a slowburn romance and an action-packed mystery. <br>D is so freaking cool, and the things he can do, felt real. <br>I have no clue whether this is how hitmen operate, but the whole story was so well-written and gripping, that I had no issues believing that D was a 'real' person. I loved how hardcore he was, and even though his moral compass is sort of skewed, and he acts like a machine, this dude was just... AWESOME.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1476863582ra/20889046.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>They go on the run together until the trial, and hole up in different places, while getting to know each other. <br>D's origin story is heartbreaking, but Jack just keeps digging and nagging and being Jack, that slowly but surely, D opens up. <br><br>I really loved the development between them, and I loved the 'doubts' Jack had later on, since that felt real as well, considering how they met and the high pressure situation they were in.<br>There wasn't a lot of action when they were holed up, but the pressure was still ON, and you could <b>FEEL</b> it in their interactions and their personalities.<br>Also MAJOR props to X and Churchill! These two were FREAKING amazing, supporting characters, and Ms. Seville did an amazing job of keeping me on my toes during the whole story in a: who-can-you-trust-limbo?<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1476873581ra/20890931.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>The only problem I had with this book, were the smexy times. The rest of the book and the characters were so fleshed-out and developed, BUT the smexy times were lacking.<br>It read like there was next to no prep, they have sex without a condom and the smexy times weren't really described, but skipped over, and that was annoying since the rest was so well-done.<br>BUT I loved the ending, I loved Jack and D and I loved the development of the story, most of this book was just freaking amazing.<br><br>There is no doubt in my mind that the next book in the series (the full novel, not the short stories) will be a one-click-buy for me. Come on Ms. Seville, we need more fantastic Jack and hardcore D!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1406059679ra/10495610.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_503954846" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/503954846" />
    <a title="Gina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10220350-gina"><img alt="Gina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1381582790p2/10220350.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/503954846?book_show_action=true">Jan 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Gina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Gina" href="/user/show/10220350-gina">Gina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Gina by: </span>
      Kathleen Young
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10220350-gina?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10220350-gina?shelf=best-of-the-best">best-of-the-best</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10220350-gina?shelf=m-m">m-m</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer503954846" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5209027180132600157">This story was amazing! Absolutely, positively OMG I actually hugged my ereader after AMAZING!!! And I actually considered staring over immediately and reading it again! (yes, I think I may have some obsessive compulsive issues as well)<br/><br/>This was about Jack a maxillofacial surgeon who works at Johns Hopkins In Baltimore, MD (which is quite cool for me because i actually have one, and he works at Johns Hopkins). Leaving work one day he witnesses a woman getting murdered, he hides so no one sees him</span>
  <span id="freeText5209027180132600157" style="display:none">This story was amazing! Absolutely, positively OMG I actually hugged my ereader after AMAZING!!! And I actually considered staring over immediately and reading it again! (yes, I think I may have some obsessive compulsive issues as well)<br><br>This was about Jack a maxillofacial surgeon who works at Johns Hopkins In Baltimore, MD (which is quite cool for me because i actually have one, and he works at Johns Hopkins). Leaving work one day he witnesses a woman getting murdered, he hides so no one sees him and watches the whole thing. He reports it to the authorities, they put him in protective custody so the crime organization who committed the murder can't get him. Now Jack in quite likable, friendly, he takes care of himself, outgoing, people like him and he is attractive, not snobby or condensing because he is a big time doctor. Someone i could honestly see myself wanting to hang out with. But Jack found his life boring and mundane, the only thing that kept him company at night was whatever movie was on TCM.<br><br>Now D is a hit man, and he is being blackmailed to kill Jack (I am not going to tell you how because you are going to read the book). But D decides not to, but he just can't walk away because he knows someone else will if he won't. So D forces Jack to go on the run with him. And so off they go!<br><br>Now what totally made D believable for me was the way the writer introduced me to him. The fact that he is gay never comes up till later, so i put it out of my mind honestly. What I was introduced to was a man who was barely existing, someone who didn't feel human anymore. And while he and Jack were on the run D hardly communicates with Jack, all Jack gets are grunts and stares most of the time, and the writer let's you into D's head to see how difficult and how tortured D really is. <br><br>Now as the story moves along D and Jack get closer and to be honest I can't see how the writer is going to get them "together" honestly. And then that magic moment happens...a single touch between them, a seemingly innocent touch and my heart goes all a flutter! (boy am I easy...lol). <br><br>The other thing I liked about this story is D is not your typical hero, he is a hit man, normally he is the bad guy in the story. And what I liked was how dark, tortured and honestly scary D was. While he definitely evolved in this story, parts of his personality never changed. While he opened up to Jack more and more and learned how to share his feelings and emotions, he was still a brooding, tough, scary don't want to meet him in a dark alley guy. So the fact that he just happened to be gay i found totally believable.<br><br>This story was action packed, it moved along fast, I never skipped a page or a paragraph it kept me glued to my chair. The chemistry between Jack and D I could feel, and the sex was hot and beautiful (yes, beautiful). And every time I see chocolate covered cherries i am going to think of this story (no I am not going to mention why because you are going to read the book remember).<br><br>I am happy....<br><br>Re-read November 2013<br><br>I just wanted to say this is the first book I have re-read and OMG I loved it just as much the second time around. I want to thank Macky and Tina for the awesome BR. This book did not have one slow moment for me, it moved along and I was always at the edge of my seat. I had forgotten so much of this book and now I am swooning all over again!!!!<br><br><a href="http://s1274.photobucket.com/user/funnygirl797/media/emoticons/brlove_zps506b9d72.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/461234.gif" alt=" photo brlove_zps506b9d72.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="5209027180132600157" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer166896066288834534"><blockquote>
<b>My impression reading this book?</b><br/><br/>It's like watch a very good action movie!!!</blockquote><br/><br/><b>Jack</b> <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380341320ra/697505.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>He is a very talented surgeon in the witness protection program. He saw a murder, and have no choice... he must testify against one of the most powerful and danger criminal organization.<br/><br/><b>D</b> <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/95216.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>(yeah, a letter... his name you will know only after a while) <br/>He is a hit man. <br/>Incredible cliché (sorry) but the better way to describe him is: a assassin with conscience.   <span id="freeText166896066288834534" style="display:none"><blockquote>
<b>My impression reading this book?</b><br><br>It's like watch a very good action movie!!!</blockquote><br><br><b>Jack</b> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380341320ra/697505.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>He is a very talented surgeon in the witness protection program. He saw a murder, and have no choice... he must testify against one of the most powerful and danger criminal organization.<br><br><b>D</b> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/95216.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>(yeah, a letter... his name you will know only after a while) <br>He is a hit man. <br>Incredible cliché (sorry) but the better way to describe him is: a assassin with conscience. He pick his jobs, and use his "god/evil" judgment to decide who must die by his hands.<br><br><b>The plot and the writing </b> is amazing! I love the suspense and the action! There are so many facts, secondary characters, and the main characters running against time! Everything was breathless!<br><br>I must say also something about the different point of views (POV). Both Jack and D will narrate, and the different POV were perfect! This is one of the rare books I found were when the POV chance also the mind of the writer is different! I hate two narrator thinking identical figures of speech (for example) and little details like that made me love the reading.<br><br>It was a very pleasurable reading, and regardless the action it's also a <u>very romantic story.</u> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/39031.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Both men are very strong and the romance is not something easy to them... so when start it will be heartbreaking! <br><br><b>So, 5 stars. Amazing book! I would love to see it as a movie!</b> <br><br><u>BTW</u>, to read more about Jack and D you can <a href="http://www.janesevillebooks.com/webstories.html" rel="nofollow noopener">check the writer's blog</a><br></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer151628083" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10904101694631373157"><b>Wow! Um...just, WOW</b><br/><br/>This book has <i>everything</i> in it: mystery and intrigue, romance and great sexual tension, action and suspense. And lots of sex! D, a big, bad ass hit man being forced to kill Jack, state's witness and former practicing doctor. Well, things don't exactly turn out as planned. <br/><br/>In the beginning, I immediately loved Jack because he reminded me a lot of myself. Especially when he had to nurse D back to health and how he always asking D a bunch of questions. D would have went ahead and</span>
  <span id="freeText10904101694631373157" style="display:none"><b>Wow! Um...just, WOW</b><br /><br />This book has <i>everything</i> in it: mystery and intrigue, romance and great sexual tension, action and suspense. And lots of sex! D, a big, bad ass hit man being forced to kill Jack, state's witness and former practicing doctor. Well, things don't exactly turn out as planned. <br /><br />In the beginning, I immediately loved Jack because he reminded me a lot of myself. Especially when he had to nurse D back to health and how he always asking D a bunch of questions. D would have went ahead and killed me because I never would have known when to shut my mouth. But somewhere in the middle of all this, I totally fell in love with D. He was such a passionate man and all he needed was Jack to dig in and open up that vault he had sealed tightly shut for so many years. I loved seeing how D slowly opened up and shared little pieces of himself at a time with Jack. It was very endearing and just made me want to reach out and give him a big hug. Jack was right there and able to look past D's rough and tough exterior and <i>see</i> the real man inside.<br /><br />Great book!</span>
  <a data-text-id="10904101694631373157" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('DQv31OZUV8g29pfbp1bAYW3Z/QpDipXAp+Ua3QC8G9iU/OOuArL0YHAlxONwbeZXx9+hnRjntridh2HaCfRgww==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer8023899398372715849">Jane Seville is an author living in Columbus, OH. She enjoys reading and writing about good-looking men doing naughty things to each other. She grew up around gay men; her mother directed the local gay men's chorus. Then she went off to a women's college, where as you might guess, she was surrounded by gay women. Despite not being gay herself, Jane has always had a deep connection to the gay right</span>
  <span id="freeText8023899398372715849" style="display:none">Jane Seville is an author living in Columbus, OH. She enjoys reading and writing about good-looking men doing naughty things to each other. She grew up around gay men; her mother directed the local gay men's chorus. Then she went off to a women's college, where as you might guess, she was surrounded by gay women. Despite not being gay herself, Jane has always had a deep connection to the gay rights' movement and continues to do whatever she can to help its advancement.<br /><br />Jane loves cooking, VH1 pop culture shows, inventing her own craft projects and walking her Newfoundland.</span>
